    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer10951568221907620745">Who cut off Medusa's head? Who was raised by a she-bear? Who tamed Pegasus? It takes a demigod to know, and Percy Jackson can fill you in on the all the daring deeds of Perseus, Atalanta, Bellerophon, and the rest of the major Greek heroes. Told in the funny, irreverent style readers have come to expect from Percy, ( I've had some bad experiences in my time, but the heroes</span>
  <span id="freeText10951568221907620745" style="display:none">Who cut off Medusa's head? Who was raised by a she-bear? Who tamed Pegasus? It takes a demigod to know, and Percy Jackson can fill you in on the all the daring deeds of Perseus, Atalanta, Bellerophon, and the rest of the major Greek heroes. Told in the funny, irreverent style readers have come to expect from Percy, ( I've had some bad experiences in my time, but the heroes I'm going to tell you about were the original old school hard luck cases. They boldly screwed up where no one had screwed up before. . .) and enhanced with vibrant artwork by Caldecott Honoree John Rocco, this story collection will become the new must-have classic for Rick Riordan's legions of devoted fans--and for anyone who needs a hero. So get your flaming spear. Put on your lion skin cape. Polish your shield and make sure you've got arrows in your quiver. We're going back about four thousand years to decapitate monsters, save some kingdoms, shoot a few gods in the butt, raid the Underworld, and steal loot from evil people. Then, for dessert, we'll die painful tragic deaths. Ready? Sweet. Let's do this.</span>

<div id="review_1097308924" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1097308924" />
    <a title="Muse-ic ♬" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/36574090-muse-ic"><img alt="Muse-ic ♬" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1497741975p2/36574090.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1097308924?book_show_action=true">Nov 04, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Muse-ic ♬" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Muse-ic ♬" href="/user/show/36574090-muse-ic">Muse-ic ♬</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36574090-muse-ic?shelf=omg-dat-cover">omg-dat-cover</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36574090-muse-ic?shelf=own">own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36574090-muse-ic?shelf=mythology">mythology</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1097308924" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15628328585377867393"><br/>4.5<br/><br/>Rick's books, man!<br/>They never cease to make me laugh!<br/>Some of the sentences are pure funny, while others are simply ridiculous you just have to laugh!<br/>The sarcasm is ever present! He really lays it on thick, but I was cracking up most of the time! So it worked :D<br/><br/>Take some of these chapter titles:<br/><b>Theseus Slays the Mighty--Oh, Look! A Bunny Rabbit!<br/>Cyrene Punches a Lion (No Actual Lions Were Harmed in the Making of This Myth)<br/>Jason Finds a Rug That Really Ties the Kingdom Together</b><br/><br/>The chapter titles </span>
  <span id="freeText15628328585377867393" style="display:none"><br />4.5<br /><br />Rick's books, man!<br />They never cease to make me laugh!<br />Some of the sentences are pure funny, while others are simply ridiculous you just have to laugh!<br />The sarcasm is ever present! He really lays it on thick, but I was cracking up most of the time! So it worked :D<br /><br />Take some of these chapter titles:<br /><b>Theseus Slays the Mighty--Oh, Look! A Bunny Rabbit!<br />Cyrene Punches a Lion (No Actual Lions Were Harmed in the Making of This Myth)<br />Jason Finds a Rug That Really Ties the Kingdom Together</b><br /><br />The chapter titles are the best!<br /><br />My main criticism is that there were way too many modern references. A few of them would have been fine, but there were several per chapter. <br />For example: One time, Hermes shows up in a UPS uniform in front of Perseus who asks him the meaning of the symbols on his shirts.<br />Hermes looks down and asks what century it was, then switched back to normal Ancient Greek godly attire.<br />Gods can't time travel! I mean, sure, it was really funny, but these kinds of jokes were used a lot.<br />There were so many references to cellphones and the modern texting lingo such as "Hawt" and "LOL".<br />It was clearly targeting a younger audience.<br /><br />But it was still great! A very chill read and a great pastime. Guys I gave this 5 stars! I think that means that I liked it!<br />The illustrations were beautiful as well!<br /><br />One of my favorite aspects was the constant reference to the Oracle of Delphi and how she would give a vague prophecy, then saying <i>Thank you and have a nice day</i>.<br />I just found it funny! Like, thanks for nothing!<br /><br />This is totally irrelevant to the book itself. But I ordered this off amazon, and there was like a bite or something taken out of page 345. Like there was literally a small triangle of paper just missing from the side. Like, what??<br /><br />So go read this! Even if you haven't read the Greek Gods, though I do recommend reading that first since there were some references that would be a bit difficult to understand unless you already know the myth. <br /><br />Thank you and have a nice day ;)</span>
  <a data-text-id="15628328585377867393" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1347667785" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1347667785" />
    <a title="Darren Hagan" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/34101852-darren-hagan"><img alt="Darren Hagan" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1436632030p2/34101852.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1347667785?book_show_action=true">Jul 28, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Darren Hagan" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Darren Hagan" href="/user/show/34101852-darren-hagan">Darren Hagan</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/24621111-percy-jackson-and-the-greek-heroes">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1347667785" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13972937663505484528">This book was so freaking good!! I was a bit dubious going into it considering I don't know a huge amount of Greek heroes, but the stories were told in such a funny and engaging way that it didn't really matter that I didn't know the heroes. It was literally "laugh out loud" funny. <br/><br/>It was also really educational, and the humour just made it fun to learn. Obviously it's a middle grade series, so Riordan uses a lot of modern references to keep the intended audience interested, such as saying that </span>
  <span id="freeText13972937663505484528" style="display:none">This book was so freaking good!! I was a bit dubious going into it considering I don't know a huge amount of Greek heroes, but the stories were told in such a funny and engaging way that it didn't really matter that I didn't know the heroes. It was literally "laugh out loud" funny. <br /><br />It was also really educational, and the humour just made it fun to learn. Obviously it's a middle grade series, so Riordan uses a lot of modern references to keep the intended audience interested, such as saying that the Greek Gods probably spend a lot of time Googling themselves, and <br />this text conversation between Zeus and Helios where Zeus uses the word "Totes", but those were the parts that made me laugh the most.<br /><br />Anyway yeah its a great book. It's probably more appealing to the hardcore Percy Jackson fans like myself though. It helped to pull me out of my slump a little bit though so thumbs up to that :D</span>
  <a data-text-id="13972937663505484528" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1405754796" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15155689039185979647">If anything, I think I may have liked Heroes better than <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20829994.Percy_Jackson_s_Greek_Gods__A_Percy_Jackson_and_the_Olympians_Guide_' title='Percy Jackson's Greek Gods (A Percy Jackson and the Olympians Guide) by Rick Riordan' rel='nofollow noopener'>Percy Jackson's Greek Gods</a>. That's more do to subject matter than the writing. The heroes in this book lead very exciting lives, and Riordan gives vivid and very detailed retellings of each. I also appreciated the variety he brought. Sure, no book of mythical Greek heroes would be complete without Theseus, Perseus, Jason and Heracles, and they're all in here. But he also includes Otrera and Cyrene, women I'm fairly certain I'd never heard </span>
  <span id="freeText15155689039185979647" style="display:none">If anything, I think I may have liked Heroes better than <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20829994.Percy_Jackson_s_Greek_Gods__A_Percy_Jackson_and_the_Olympians_Guide_" title="Percy Jackson's Greek Gods (A Percy Jackson and the Olympians Guide) by Rick Riordan" rel="nofollow noopener">Percy Jackson's Greek Gods</a>. That's more do to subject matter than the writing. The heroes in this book lead very exciting lives, and Riordan gives vivid and very detailed retellings of each. I also appreciated the variety he brought. Sure, no book of mythical Greek heroes would be complete without Theseus, Perseus, Jason and Heracles, and they're all in here. But he also includes Otrera and Cyrene, women I'm fairly certain I'd never heard of before. Maybe the most valuable thing about this book is how incredibly in depth Riordan goes on every single story. Yes, that may mean starting a few generations back to give the proper context, and I greatly appreciate that. Percy's snarky voice aside, that makes Heroes and Gods both pretty valuable collections of mythology.</span>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('nLsBcwYEJCI/IroIssbFBkc7mCuweO7mxdM7/O/sULTJQnPkJRC3sIHJcjbC3T74HBDpxSO+a7kc9Z9ZOjL2Yg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('AWs0v7o73ZPbvRJl6W39bFeCkOBjpTtpKzyPKXRReERUkkYomS9OAWVW2luZdgaSDKnhDvBjvjbyGiuMoY/ekg==')})
  }
//]]>
